Injongo ye yaseMzantsi Afrika kukuvelisa umthombo omnye wenkcazelo malunga neenkonzo ezinikwa ngurhulumente waseMzantsi Afrika . .
Le website ijolise ekubeni inciphise umsantsa wokwahluka okukhoyo phakathi kwabantu abanikwe amandla kunye nabo bangenamandla , phakathi koqoqosho lokuqala kunye nolwesibini . .
Le website ilungenelelo olubaluleke kakhulu olujonge ekuqinisekiseni ukuba abemi banako ukunxulumana norhulumente . .
I ijolise kubasebenzisi abangabemi baseMzantsi Afrika kuzo zonke iindawo zelizwe , amashishini okanye imibutho yaseMzantsi Afrika , ekhoyo okanye enokubakhona , kunye nabemi nemibutho ekwamanye amazwe , edinga iinkonzo kurhulumente waseMzantsi Afrika . .
Icandelo elingundoqo labasebenzisi libandakanya izilamlisi , ezifana naMaziko abahlali eenkonzo ngeeNkonzo , abizwa ngokuba zii Community Centres ( MPCCs ) , aBasebenzi boPhuhliso loLuntu , ekuthiwa zii Development Workers ( CDWs ) kunye neZiko lokuTsalela uMnxeba ekuthiwa yi Pele Gateway Call Centre , eziyakuncedisa ekuphembeleleni ukusetyenziswa kwe ngabo bangakwaziyo ukusebenzisa i nqo . .
Imiba echatshazelwa yinkcazelo ekwi .
Inkcazelo ngeenkonzo zikarhulumente .
I iqulathe inkcazelo ngeenkonzo zikarhulumente ezinikwa kwinqanaba likarhulumente welizwe . .
Inkcazelo yeenkonzo yahlulahlulwe yangamacandelo aziintlobo zeenkonzo ezintathu : .
Iinkonzo zabantu : iinkonzo zabemi baseMzantsi Afrika eziququzelelwe ngokweziganeko zobomi .
Iinkonzo zemibutho : iinkonzo ezingqamene nemibutho kunye namashishini .
Iinkonzo zabantu bamazwe angaphandle : inkcazelo engqaliselwe abemi abaphuma kwamanye amazwe abadinga iinkonzo ezibandakanyekayo kurhulumente waseMzantsi Afrika . .
Icandelo ngalinye kula liphinde lakhiwa ngohlobo oluhambisana nendlela yokulandelelana kweziganeko zobomi ( iziganeko ezineempawu ezithile kubomi bommi okanye beshishini ) . .
Iziganeko zobomi ziphinda zahlulahlulwe ngokwezigaba zobomi . .
Inkcazelo kwinkonzo nganye ilungiselelwe ngokwemiba esisiseko esixhenxe , eyile : inkcazelo , inkqubo emayilandelwe , imithetho esetyenziswayo , ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo , iindleko , iifom ezigcwaliswayo , kunye neenkcukacha zonxulumano . .
Inkcazelo eyayameneyo .
Eli candelo le website , eliboniswe kumgca wokukhangela osekunene , liqulathe unxulumaniso kwii ezayameneyo kweso siganeko sobomi . .
Iilwimi .
Oluhlobo lwe lulungiselelwe iilwimi ezilishumi elinanye njengesiNgesi , isibhulu , isiNdebele , isiXhosa , isiZulu , isiPedi , isiSuthu , isiTsonga , isiSwati , isiVenda kunye nesiTswana .
Inkcazelo yenkonzo ngokwemvelaphi ibhalwe nge , ize ke emva koko iguqulelwe kwezinye iilwimi . .
Inkcazelo yeenkonzo ekwezinye iilwimi ifakwa kwi emva kokuba iguquliwe . .
Ezinye izibakala ze .
Sebenzisa iphepha elithi Nxulumana nathi ukuze wenze iziphawulo okanye ubuzise nge yeeNkonzo zikaRhulumente . .
Unxulumaniso lwe www.gov.za lufikelelisa kwiphepha lokungena le kaRhulumente waseMzantsi Afrika , elifikelelisa kule webiste ( i yeeNkonzo zikaRhulumente ) kunye ne yeNkcazelo kaRhulumente ( www.info.gov.za ) . .
Imephu yesiza ilumelo lwembonakalo yamehlo yolwakhiwo nocwangciso lwe . .
Inikezelwa ngokokulandelelana kobume nogunyaziso , nto leyo ecubungula inkcazelo yesiza ibeyimiba yezihloko ezingqaliseka ngokwandayo . .
Ngoko ke iyakunceda ukwazi ukuzifundisa malunga nendlela ekucwangciswe ngayo imiba equlathwe kwi . .
Iphepha lokufikelelisa kwinkcazelo ye linika udweliso lwezona nkonzo kufikelelwa kuzo kakhulu . .
Ezi ngeniso zifikelelisa kwiinkonzo ezintlanu ezizezona zityelelwa kakhulu ngabasebenzisi . .
Olu dweliso luqhelaniswa nemeko yezibalo zesitatistiksi samaphepha atyelelweyo . .
Ibhokisi yokufunisa iyafumaneka kuwo onke amaphepha kwi . .
Xa ungenisa amagama okufunisa , kuyakufuniswa ngala magama kuyo yonke i . .
Kwakhona , usengangenisa ufuniso olulolona lunenkqubela nolukwizinga eliphezulu ngokukhetha unxulumaniso lwe search . .
Olu hlobo lokufunisa lufunisa ngenkcazelo kwezinye ii zikarhulumente . .
Unxulumaniso kwii zangaphandle luboniswa ngamagama athi , ' outside link - opens in new window ' , ayakubonakala kwibhokisi xa i yakho igqithiselwa kunxulumaniso . .
I iyakuvula isikroba esitsha sokukhangela . .
Ukulandelelana kwezihlandlo zokufaka inkcazelo yakutshanje .
I imana ifakwa inkcazelo entsha . .
Umgaqo wethu kukunika inkcazelo njengoko imana ifumaneka kwaye naxa ifumaneka . .
Nangona kunjalo , abavelisi be yeeNkonzo zikaRhulumente abanakunika isiqinisekiso ngobutsha benkcazelo epapashwa kwezinye ii esinxulumana nazo . .
Jonga icandelo elithi , iiMeko neMiqathango , kumhlathi 4.3 . .
Ubunikazi benkcazelo .
Amasebe karhulumente athabathela kuwo ubunikazi benkcazelo yawo kwi . .
Lo msebenzi wanikwa oomanejala bonxulumano , abanoxanduva lwenkcazelo epapashwa kwi . .
I Communications ( GCIS ) inoxanduva lokuphatha nokulawula ukuhlanganiswa kwemiba equlathwe kwi . .
Ubume bohlobo lwemiqulu .
Obona bume bohlobo lwemiqulu bufumaneka kakhulu ngenkcazelo kwi yi . .
Kodwa ke , iindidi ze zemiqulu ( umzekelo , iMithetho , iifom ) ziyanikwa ukuze kugcinwe uqobo loyilo lwemiqulu . .
Ukuze uvule imiqulu ye , kufuneka ufakelwe kwikhompiyutha yakho i Acrobat Reader 4 okanye uhlobo olungaphezulu kwayo . .
Iya kuvulela imiqulu nqo kwisikhangeli sakho . .
Ngamanye amaxesha kuthabatha ixesha elide ukuvula imiqulu ye . .
Kule meko ke , sicebisa ukuba uyithulele kwikhompiyutha yakho , uze ke uyivulele kuyo . .
cebisa ukuthulela imiqulu kwikhompiyutha yakho . .
Xa usebenzisa isiHloli se ( Internet Explorer ) njengesikhangeli sakho : .
Ngokusebenzisa i yakho , cofa ngasekunene kumqulu ofuna ukuwuthula . .
Kwiintlobo zezihloko ezidweliswe ngokuhlayo , khetha iqhosha elithi : ' Save target as ' . .
Kwibhokisi ethi ' Save as ' , khetha indawo ofuna ukugcina kuyo lo mqulu kwidiski yakho yokugcina inkcazelo kwaye ucofe iqhosha elithi ' Save ' . .
Ifayili iyakuthulelwa kwindawo oyichazileyo . .
Vula isikroba se Reader yakho , uze ke uvule imiqulu oyithobileyo . .
Xa usebenzisa i njengesikhangeli sakho : .
Ngokusebenzisa i yakho , yithi cebu kwaye ucofe ( kwicala lokucofa elingasekhohlo le ) kwisinxulumanisi somqulu ofuna ukuwugcina . .
Kwibhokisi ethi ' Save As ' , khetha indawo ofuna ukugcina kuyo lo mqulu kwidiski yakho yokugcina inkcazelo kwaye ucofe iqhosha elithi ' Save ' . .
Ifayili iyakuthulelwa kwindawo oyichazileyo . .
Vula isikroba se- Acrobat Reader yakho , uze uvule imiqulu oyithobileyo . .
Ingaba udinga uncedo ngeengxaki ohlangene nazo kwi ? .
Nceda unxulumane nathi ( electronic@gcis.gov.za ) ukuba ngaba udibana neengxaki nge . .
Ukubangaba iqumrhu , inkampani okanye iqumrhu elingavulelekanga alinako okanye aliyi kuwahlawula amatyala alo okanye lifezekise uxanduva lwalo ( ngenxa yokuba alikwazi ukuhlawula amatyala alo , ngenxa yokulawulwa kakubi okanye ngenxa yaso nasiphina esinye isizathu ) , uMqondisi wezoRhwebo naMashishini angalilawula ngokwasemthethweni okanye aliphelise iqumrhu loshishino . .
Iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa , naliphina ilungu lequmrhu okanye nawuphina omnye umntu onomnqweno , angenza isicelo kwiinkundla sokuba iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa lifakwe phantsi kolawulo lwasemthethweni loMqondisi okanye lipheliswe . .
Inkundla emamela esi sicelo kufuneka ibelicandelo leNkundla ePhezulu okanye iNkundla kaMantyi enamandla okumisela ubulungisa kummandla iqumrhu elikuwo okanye eliqhuba kuwo iinkonzo . .
Nazo iinkundla zingawisa umyalelo ngolu hlobo ukuba ngaba ngowona myalelo ungcono okanye ufanelekileyo kule meko . .
Ukubangaba inkundla iwisa umyalelo wokuba uMqondisi kufuneka alawule ngokusemthethweni iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa , uyakubanegunya lokuphatha imibandela yequmrhu okanye yequmrhu lokubambisa , phantsi kwemiqathango yoMthetho weeNkampani . .
Ukubangaba iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa lenza isicelo esibhaliweyo kuMqondisi , uMqondisi angalicima ubhaliso lwequmrhu okanye lwequmrhu lokubambisa ukuba ngaba wanelisekile ukuba .
isindululo esixhasa ukucinywa kobhaliso savunywa kwintlanganiso eyayiyiwe linani elivokothekileyo lamalungu equmrhu okanye equmrhu lokubambisa ; .
isindululo savunywa sisininzi samalungu awayekhona okanye awayemelwe kule ntlanganiso ; kwaye .
amanyathelo athatyathiwe malunga nayo yonke imibandela ebandakanyekayo ekufanele ngokwengqiqo kujongwane nayo phambi kokucinywa kobhaliso , kubandakanywa inkqubo eyakulandelwa malunga nempahla nezinto kunye nezinto eziluxanduva lwemfaneleko nezingamatyala equmrhu . .
Ukubangaba inkundla igqiba ekubeni iphelise iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa , iyakwenza isigqibo malunga nendlela impahla nezinto zequmrhu eziyakwahlulwa ngayo ngokulinganayo nangokufanelekileyo . .
Inkundla iyakuziqwalasela naziphina iziphakamiso ezinokuba zenziwe nguMqondisi malunga nokwabiwa kwempahla nezinto . .
Ukubangaba uMqondisi okanye iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa , naliphina ilungu lequmrhu okanye nawuphina omnye umntu onomnqweno , wenza isicelo sokuba iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa lifakwe phantsi kolawulo lwasemthethweni loMqondisi okanye lipheliswe , UMphathiswa angamisela imigaqo ekuyakulawulwa ngayo iqumrhu okanye iqumrhu lokubambisa nguMqondisi okanye eliyakupheliswa ngayo . .
UMphathiswa angachaza namandla nemisebenzi yoMqondisi , iGosa loBhaliso , iqumrhu , amalungu kunye nababandakanyeki abanomnqweno kwezi meko . .
Kwimeko yenkampani okanye yequmrhu elingavulelekanga ekuthiwa yi corporation ( CC ) , nawuphina umbandakanyeki onomnqweno , umqondisi okanye umphicothi weencwadi zemali wenkampani , i African Revenue Service ( SARS ) okanye uMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani , angenza isicelo sokuba inkampani okanye i icinywe kubhaliso . .
Umnyinyiva wokubonelela ngerhafu unikwa imibutho engajonganga kwenza nzuzo , esekelwe yinzuzo kuluntu ngokubanzi . .
Nangona kunjalo , lo mnyenyevu wokubonelela uyakufumaneka kuphela kwimibutho ehambisana nemimiselo yoMthetho weMibutho eNgajonganga kwenza Nzuzo , kunye nemithetho eyayamene nawo . .
Imibutho enqwenela ukwenza izicelo zomnyinyiva wokungabandakanywa kufanele ziwele phantsi kwelinye lala macandelo alandelayo : .
Inkampani efakwe phantsi kweCandelo 21 loMthetho weeNkampani Inkampani yeCandelo 21 inemimiselo kunye nemigaqo yokumanyana njengemiqulu yokuyiseka kwaye ibhalisiwe kuMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani . .
Iqumrhu lokugcina ngentembeko elinomqulu wokuliseka kunye nencwadi yesivumelwano sasemthethweni sentembeko , esibhaliswe kwiNqununu yeNkundla ePhezulu . .
Iqumrhu labantu . .
Iqumrhu labantu abahlangene ngokuzithandela elilawulwa ngumgaqo . .
Xa imiqulu yokuseka ingahambisani nemimiselo yeCandelo 30 loMthetho weMibutho eNgajonganga kwenza Nzuzo , isicelo kufuneka sikhatshwe sisibhengezo sesithembiso esibhaliweyo esisayinwe ngumenzi . .
Uyakuthi ke umnyinyiva wangaphambili uqhubeke ukusebenza kude kube leloxesha apho umenzi ayakube azisiwe yi African Revenue Service ( SARS ) ngesigqibo ngokomthetho omtsha . .
Imibutho okungokunje enganikwanga umnyinyiva ogunyazisiweyo wokungabandakanywa kwirhafu yengeniso , ingathumela ifom yesicelo egcwalisiweyo ehamba nemiqulu yokuxhasa eyimfuneko , ndawonye nesibhengezo sesithembiso esibhaliweyo nesisayiniweyo , apho abantu abenza lo msebenzi ngentembeko bathembisa ngokuhambisana nemimiselo yeCandelo 30 loMthetho weMibutho eNgajonganga kwenza Nzuzo . .
Le miqulu yokuxhasa ilandelayo kufuneka ikhaphe isicelo : .
inkampani : Faka ikopi yeMimiselo kunye neMigaqo yokuManyana ( ebandakanya iikopi zazo zonke izindululo ezizodwa ezibhalisiweyo ezilungisa imimiselo kunye nemigaqo ) .
iqumrhu lokugcina ngentembeko : Faka ikopi yeencwadi zezivumelwano zasemthethweni zentembeko kunye nazo naziphina iincwadi zezivumelwano zasemthethweni ezilandelayo zokulungisa .
iqumrhu labantu : Faka ikopi yomgaqo wakutshanje . .
Imibutho esekwe ngenjongo ephambili yokunika izipho zemali yokufunda ngenxa yokugqwesa , iibhasari kunye nezipho zokufunda , uphando kunye nokufundisa , kufuneka , ngaphezulu kwale miqulu ingentla , igcwalise iSibhengezo seSithembiso eSibhaliweyo ekuthiwa yi 3 Written Undertaking . .
Izikolo zoluntu kunye nezizimeleyo ( ezabucala ) , amaziko emfundo ephakamileyo , amaziko emfundo esisiseko noqeqesho lwabantu abadala ( i ) , ndawonye namaziko emfundo noqeqesho oluqhubekayo ( i ) , kufuneka zifake ikopi yesatifikethi sobhaliso esikhutshwe nguGunyaziwe obandakanyekayo weMfundo . .
Inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu luxanduva lokunika omnye umntu , umzekelo umntwana ongekabinamalungelo okuzithabathela izigqibo ngokwasemthethweni , ukutya , indlu , impahla yokunxiba , imfundo kunye nonakekelo lonyango , okanye ukulungiselela omnye umntu iindlela nezinto eziyimfuneko ukuze anikwe ezi zinto zidingekayo kwimpilo yakhe . .
Olu xanduva lwasemthethweni lokunika inkxaso lubizwa ngokuba ' luxanduva lokuxhasa okanye ' luxanduva lokusapota ' . .
Ngubani ekufuneka akhuphe inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu ( isapoti ) ? .
Uxanduva lokusapota lusekelwe kubudlelwane begazi , ukwamkelwa komntwana abengowomnye umntu okanye abantu ngokusemthethweni okanye kwimeko yokokuba aba bantu batshatile . .
Umntwana kufuneka asapotwe okanye axhaswe .
Ngabazali bakhe , nokuba batshatile , bayahlalisana , bahlukene okanye baqhawule umtshato ( badivosile ) , kubandakanywa abazali abamkele umntwana wabangowabo ngokusemthethweni ; kunye / okanye .
Ootatomkhulu noomakhulu bakhe , nokuba ngaba abazali bomntwana babetshatile okanye babengatshatanga . .
Kodwa ke oku kwahluka ngokwemeko ngemeko . .
Uxanduva lokusapota ilungu losapho ( lefemeli ) aliqingqelwa nje kuphela ukusapota umntwana . .
Naliphina ilungu lefemeli , nokuba lineminyaka yobudala engakanani na , lingacela naliphina ilungu lefemeli lilisapote okanye lilixhase , kodwa ke xa ngaba le miqathango mibini ilandelayo ifezekisiwe : .
Iilungu lefemeli elibanga isapoti alinako ukuzisapota ngokwalo . .
Ilungu lefemeli ekucelwa kulo isapoti alinakoyisakala ukusikhupha esi sapoti sibangwayo . .
Zeziphi iinkcitho ezingabangwa ? .
Ungabanga isapoti esiqiqileyo esiyimfuneko ukuze unike umntwana okanye omnye umntu onelungelo lokusapotwa indlela yokuphila nokukhula okufanelekileyo . .
Oku kubandakanya ukunika izinto ezidingekayo empilweni ezifana nokutya , impahla yokunxiba kunye nendlu , ndawonye nokuhlawuwulela imfundo efanelekileyo . .
Inkundla ingayalela nokuba utata womntwana enze igalelo kwintlawulo yeendleko zokulungiselelwa komntwana kunye nenkxaso ukusukela kumhla wokuzalwa komntwana ukuyakutsho kumhla wokunikwa komyalelo wesapoti . .
Inkundla inganika nomyalelo wokuhlawulwa kweendleko zonyango okanye ingayalela ukuba umntwana abhaliswe phantsi kwesikim sonyango somnye wabazali njengomntu oxhomekekileyo . .
Ukwenzela ukuba inkundla ikwazi ukukhupha umyalelo wesapoti ofanelekileyo , bobabini abazali mabanike inkundla ubungqina beendleko zabo . .
Imbono yakho ngokuziphatha komnye umzali ayilichaphazeli ilungelo labantwana bakho lokufumana isapoti . Kukwafuneka usihlawule isapoti , nokuba ngaba omnye lo umzali .
uphinde watshata ; .
uhambisana ( unobudlelwane ) nomnye umntu ; .
akavumi ukuba ubone abantwana ; okanye .
ukuba ngaba nawuphina umbandakanyeki emva kwexesha labanye abantwana . .
Uxanduva lwakho lokuhlawula isapoti kunye nelungelo lakho lokufikelela ebantwaneni bakho yimibandela emibini eyahlukene kakhulu kwaye ayingqamananga tu . .
Ngaphezu koko , abantwana bakhe nawuphina umzali abaluchaphazeli uxanduva lokusapota . .
Kodwa ke , nangona kunjalo , imali yesapoti ingalungiswa ukuba ngaba omnye umbandakanyeki uzisa isicelo esinjalo . .
Inkqubo emayilandelwe .
Yenza isicelo sesapoti kwinkundla kamantyi ekwisithili ohlala kuso . .
Ukubangaba uyathandabuza , inkundla yendawo ohlala kuyo iyakukuxelela ukuba usenze kweyiphina inkundla isicelo sesapoti . .
Yiya kwinkundla efanelekileyo uze ugcwalise kwaye uhambise iFom A , ethi : Isicelo somyalelo wenkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu . .
Ngaphezulu kwefom oyigcwalisileyo , hambisa ubungqina bengeniso yakho yenyanga kunye neenkcitho , obufana neerisiti zokuthenga ukutya , umbane kunye neentlawulo zeemali ezibizwayo zerenti okanye beentlawulo zeemali ezibizwayo zerenti . .
Inkundla iyakubeka umhla ekuyakufuneka wena nomphenduli ( umntu ofuna ahlawule isapoti ) niye ngawo enkundleni . .
Igosa lesapoti kunye nomphandi bayakuphanda isibango sakho kwaye bajonge iimeko zakho . .
Inkundla iyakukhuphela umphenduli ( lo mntu kwenziwa kuye isibango ) isamani ( incwadi eyalela umntu ukuba aye enkundleni ) ukuze aye kuvela enkundleni ngomhla ochaziweyo ukuze kuxoxwe ngalo mbandela . .
Umphenduli ke angakhetha ukuba avume ukuhlawula esi sapoti ngale ndlela ibangwa ngayo , okanye aye kuphikisana nalo mba enkundleni . .
Ukubangaba umphenduli uyavuma ukuhlawula isapoti njengoko sibangwa , umantyi uyakuphonononga imiqulu efanelekileyo . .
Uyakuthi ke akhuphe umyalelo , kwaye angagqiba ekubeni enze njalo ngaphandle kokufuna ukuba ababandakanyeki bavele enkundleni . .
Ukubangaba umntu ekuthiwa unoxanduva lokufaneleka ahlawule isapoti akakuvumi ukukhutshwa komyalelo , kufuneka avele enkundleni , apho kuyakumanyelwa khona ubungqina bababandakanyeki bobabini nobamangqina babo . .
Ukubangaba inkundla ifumanise lo mntu enoxanduva lokufaneleka ahlawule isapoti , iyakwenza umyalelo wemali yesapoti ekufuneka ihlawulwe . .
Inkundla iyakuqulungqa nokuba zenziwe ninina , njanina iintlawulo zesapoti . .
Inkundla ingayalela ukuba imali yesapoti ihlawulwe ngenye yezi ndlela zilandelayo : .
Kwi kamantyi ekwindawo umntu ahlala kuyo okanye kuyo nayiphina enye i karhulumente echongelwe le meko .
Kwi yebhanki okanye yequmrhu lokwakha echongwe ngulo mntu ubandakanyekayo .
Nqo kulo mntu ufaneleke afumane le mali .
Ngomyalelo oyalela ukuba umqashi womntu onoxanduva lokufaneleka ahlawule isapoti axhuzule intlawulo yesapoti nqo kumvuzo womqeshwa , ngokuhambisana noMthetho omtsha weNkxaso yokuNakekela omnye umntu .
Le fom yesicelo kufuneka igcwaliswe ngumenzi , hayi umntu wesithathu - kungenjalo isicelo asiyi kuqwalaselwa . .
Nceda ubhekise kwisikhokelo sesicelo ukuze sikuncede ngenkqubo yelayisensi . .

khangela ibhokisi yokuhlola yoMngenisi wempahla , phantsi kobhaliso . .

ikhowudi yesitalato sommandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini .
ngubani oyakubanoxanduva lokubhala nokuthumela imiqulu kwi African Revenue Service ; kunye nokuba .
ingaba nguwe oyakubhala kwaye athumele le miqulu , okanye ingaba kuyakutyunjwa i ukuze yenze oku , na . .
Icandelo elithi Authority to Apply ( Igunya lokwenza isicelo ) maligcwaliswe ngumntu ( ongumnikazi ozimele yedwa , umqondisi , oogxa bentsebenziswano , ilungu , ilungu eliphathiswe iqumrhu ngentembeko , okanye umntu ophethe ishishini ) owenza isicelo sokubhalisela ukuba ngumngenisi wempahla nezinto ezithile elizweni . .
Igama lomenzi okanye igama lobhaliso lweshishini , hayi igama lorhwebo , kufuneka liboniswe kweli candelo . .
apho kubonakala khona inkwenkwezana ekuthiwa yi ( * ) , susa nayiphina efaneleke njalo . .
Kwicandelo le Declaration ( ISibhengezo ) , faka oku kulandelayo : .
oonobumba bamagama okuqala kunye nefani yomntu owenza isicelo sokunikwa ilayisensi . .
isikhundla somntu owenza isicelo , umzekelo , uMqondisi , uManejala , uMnikazi .
lo mntu wenza isicelo kufuneka atyikitye ( asayine ) ifom yesicelo .
umhla esisayinwe ngawo esi sicelo .
indawo esisayinelwe kuyo esi sicelo .
Gcwalisa ifom yesicelo uze uyise kwi ekufuphi yeMirhumo yeMpahla eNgena eLizweni kunye neRhafu yeMpahla neZinto kunye neeLayisensi ezithile , ye African Revenue Service . .
Faka iikopi eziluqobo lwazo okanye eziqinisekisiweyo zale miqulu ilandelayo : .
iphepha lemvume ( ipemethe ) yeSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini ukuba iyabandakanyeka .
iindlela zokubala ukuba ngaba wenza isicelo phantsi komba wokubuyiselwa imali ku 607.04.10(02) , 607.04.10(03) , 607.04.10(09) naku 607.04.10(12) .
iincwadi zezazisi xa umntu engummi waseMzantsi Afrika .
imiqulu yepaspoti kwimeko yomntu ongahlali kweli lizwe .
umntu ubuqu bakhe .
oogxa bentsebenziswano kwiqumrhu elingavulelekanga okanye kwiqumrhu lokugcina ngentembeko - onke amalungu , oogxa bentsebenziswano okanye amalungu aphathiswe iqumrhu ngentembeko .
inkampani - bonke abaqondisi , kubandakanywa umqondisi olawulayo kunye nomqondisi wezemali . .
Umenzi , hayi umntu wesithathu , kufuneka ibenguye ogcwalise ifom yesicelo ( DA 185 ) , kungenjalo isicelo asiyi kuqwalaselwa . .
Kwicandelo ( A ) elithi Client Types ( Iintlobo zeeKlayenti ) , khangela ibhokisi yokuhlola iMali eBuyiswayo , kwicandelo lobhaliso . .
Kwicandelo elithi Trading particulars ( Iinkcukacha zokuRhweba ) ( Uhlobo lweKlayenti II ) , kufuneka uchaze : .
igama lokurhweba leshishini lakho .
igama nenombolo yesitalato seshishini elibuyiselwayo .
igama kunye nenombolo yomgangatho wesakhiwo ekuqhutyelwa kuso eli shishini .
ummandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini .
isixeko okanye idolophu elimi kuyo ishishini .
ikhowudi yesitalato sommandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini . .
Icandelo elithi Authority to apply ( Igunya lokwenza isicelo ) , maligcwaliswe ngumenzi ( UMnikazi oZimele Yedwa , UMqondisi , Oogxa beNtsebenziswano , iLungu , iLungu eliPhathiswe iQumrhu ngeNtembeko okanye umntu ophethe naliphina elinye iqumrhu ) xa usenza isicelo sokuba ngumsebenzisi wokubuyiswa kwemali . .
Igama lomenzi okanye igama lobhaliso lweshishini , hayi igama lorhwebo , kufuneka liboniswe kweli candelo . .
Apho kubonakala khona inkwenkwezana ekuthiwa yi ( * ) , susa nayiphina efaneleke njalo . .
Kwicandelo elithi Rebate Store particulars ( Iinkcukacha zeShishini lokuBuyiswa kweMali ) , kufuneka unike : .
inkcazelo yempahla nezinto eziyakugcinwa kwishishini lokubuyiselwa imali .
izinga lemirhumo yentlawulo okanye imiba yempahla nezinto ezingeniswayo eziyakugcinwa kwishishini lokubuyiselwa imali .
imiba yokubuyiselwa imali phantsi kwamanani oludwe lwenkqubo yesi 3 , 4 , 5 kunye neyesi 6 .
inkcazelo yemveliso engeniswa kweli lizwe okanye impahla nezinto ezingeniswa kweli lizwe . .
Kwicandelo le Declaration ( Isibhengezo ) , kufuneka ufake : .
oonobumba bamagama okuqala kunye nefani yomntu owenza isicelo sokunikwa ilayisensi .
isikhundla somntu owenza isicelo , umzekelo , UMqondisi , uManejala , uMnikazi .
lo mntu wenza isicelo kufuneka atyikitye ( asayine ) ifom yesicelo .
umhla esisayinwe ngawo esi sicelo .
indawo esisayinelwe kuyo esi sicelo . .
Umenzi makase ifom egcwalisiweyo kwi ekufuphi yeMirhumo yeMpahla eNgena eLizweni kunye neRhafu yeMpahla neZinto kunye neeLayisensi ezithile , ye African Revenue Services . .
Nceda ufake iikopi eziluqobo lwazo okanye eziqinisekisiweyo zale miqulu ilandelayo : .
isatifiketi sobhaliso lweshishini njengoko sikhutshwe nguMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani okanye iNqununu yeNkundla ePhezulu kwimeko yeQumrhu lokuGcina ngeNtembeko .
isindululo okanye imvume okanye elinye igunya njengoko kubandakanyeka .
iphepha lemvume ( ipemethe ) yeSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini ukuba iyabandakanyeka .
iindlela zokubala ukuba ngaba wenza isicelo phantsi komba wokubuyiselwa imali ku 607.04.10(02) , 607.04.10(03) , 607.04.10(09) naku 607.04.10(12) .
iincwadi zezazisi xa umntu enguMmi waseMzantsi Afrika okanye iincwadi zePaspoti xa umntu engahlali kweli lizwe : .
kumntu ubuqu bakhe .
kooGxa beNtsebenziswano kwiQumrhu eliNgavulelekanga neQumrhu lokuGcina ngeNtembeko - Onke aMalungu / ooGxa beNtsebenziswano / aMalungu aPhathiswe iQumrhu ngeNtembeko .
KwiNkampani - Bonke abaqondisi , kubandakanywa uMqondisi oLawulayo kunye noMqondisi weZemali . .
Zonke izichumisi ( iifetelayisi ) ezingeniswa kweli ziphuma kwamanye amazwe , ezenziwa , eziveliswa okanye ezithengiswa eMzantsi Afrika kufuneka zibhaliswe kuMphathi woBhaliso loMthetho 36 ka 1947 ( kwi of Act 36 of 1947 ) . .
Umenzi kufuneka abengumntu ongummi ngokwasemthethweni , umzekelo : John Peter Citizen T/A Diepsloot Stud . .
Inkampani yelizwe laphesheya ayinakwenza sicelo sokubhalisa eMzantsi Afrika . .
Isicelo sokubhalisa izichumisi singenziwa kuphela yinkampani ebhaliswe kweli lizwe , ummi weRiphablikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika , okanye iqumrhu elisemthethweni elibhaliswe eMzantsi Afrika . .
Izichumisi ezikuHlelo 1 ( Group 1 ) zezo zine , i okanye i njengezona zithako ziphambili , yaye zikwabizwa ngokuba zii fertilizers . .
Ubhaliso luyakwenziwa xa ngaba ngexesha lokubhaliswa kwenzeka ezi zinto zilandelayo : .
izinto eziqulathwe sisichumisi esibandakanyekayo azohlukanga kweziya sele zibhalisiwe .
iinkcukacha kunye namagama asetyenzisiweyo avunyiweyo emibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo okanye inkonkxa akayi kutshintshwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso .
imiqathango ebekwe ngexesha lobhaliso iyalandelwa .
ubhaliso olubandakanyekayo aluyi kugqithiselwa .
ubungakanani beebhegi neenkonkxa abunakuguqulwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso . .
Isicelo sokubhaliswa kokutya kwemfuyo yasefama kunye nezichumiso siqulathe ezi zinto zilandelayo incwadi yangaphezulu esuka kumntu obhalisileyo okanye ummeli otyunjiweyo . .
Incwadi yangaphezulu kufuneka ibandakanye ezi zinto zilandelayo : .
igama lemveliso .
inombolo yobhaliso ukuba ngaba imveliso seyibhalisiwe .
isizathu sokufaka isicelo ( nokuba sisicelo esitsha , isicelo sokulungisa , isicelo sokubhalisa ufakelo ekuthiwa yi registration ) .
iincwadi zokuvuma ukuba ngaba kufuneka imvume ephuma kumntu obhalisileyo ( imvume yokubhalisa ufakelo ekuthiwa yi registration okanye imvume yokusebenzisa igama lemveliso yenye inkampani kumbhalo wokuphawula okuqulathiweyo ) .
intlawulo yesicelo echanekileyo .
iitshekhi ezithunyelwe ngokwahlukeneyo kwisicelo mazikhatshwe yincwadi echazayo ( itshekhi nee orders mazenziwe zihlawuleke kuMqondisi weZolimo ( Director : Agriculture ) .
iphepha loqulungqo . .
Hambisa ifom yesicelo kwizicelo ezitsha nakwezolungiso kubhaliso olukhoyo , kubandakanywa ukutshintsha uqulunqo . .
Hambisa iifom zesicelo kwizikhutshelo zamaphepha amabini u gcwalise iifom ngokupheleleyo , ungabhekisi kwizicelo zangaphambili , iinombolo zamaphepha okanye ezinye iimveliso ( okungenani ikopi enye yeefom zesicelo mayibenesignitsha eluqobo lwayo . .
Enye le ingayikopi ) . .
Umntu otyunjwe ngokwasemthethweni , ekufuneka ngokukhethekayo abengumntu wonxulumano loMphathi woBhaliso kwinkampani , makasayine iifom zesicelo . .
Igama nenombolo yobhaliso yemveliso mayisetyenziswe njengoko kungqaliwe kwisatifiketi sobhaliso . .
Naluphina utshintsho kwigama , nokuba luncinane kangakanani na , luyakuthathwa ngokuba sisilungiso . .
Thumela iifom zesicelo kwi yolawulo . .
Ukusa izicelo kuBacebisi boBuchwepheshe kuyakulibazisa inkqubo . .
Imibhalo engekagqitywa ( eyidrafti ) yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo : .
yihambise ngezikhutshelo zamaphepha amabini .
yihambise nge nange . .
Akukho mfuneko yokushicilela imibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo ngazo zombini ezi lwimi .
kufuneka ifundeke ngokucacileyo , kwaye ibhalwe ngokobume obuchanekileyo .
ungazifaki iinombolo kwizilumkiso neengqalelo zokuhlaba ukhangele .
zonke iinkcukacha ezikwimibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo mazingqamane nqo nezo zikwifom yesicelo . .
Zonke izichumisi ( iifetelayisi ) ezingeniswa kweli ziphuma kwamanye amazwe , ezenziwa , eziveliswa okanye ezithengiswa eMzantsi Afrika kufuneka zibhaliswe kuMphathi woBhaliso loMthetho 36 ka 1947 ( kwi Act 36 of 1947 ) . .

Izichumisi ezikuHlelo 2 zezo zinezinto eziphilayo ezincinane nezinkulu njengezona zithako ziphambili , yaye zikwabizwa ngokuba zii fertilizers . .

isatifiketi socubungulo okanye iphepha lenkcazelo . .

Imibhalo engekagqitywa ( eyidrafti ) yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo : .
yihambise ngezikhutshelo zamaphepha amabini .
yihambise nge nange . .
Akukho mfuneko yokuba imibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo ishicilelelwe ukusasazwa nemveliso ngazo zombini ezi lwimi .
kufuneka ifundeke ngokucacileyo , kwaye ibhalwe ngokobume obuchanekileyo .
ungazifaki iinombolo kwizilumkiso neengqalelo zokuhlaba ukhangele .
zonke iinkcukacha ezikwimibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo mazingqamane nqo nezo zikwifom yesicelo . .
Amalungelo abaMilisi bezityalo anikelwa kuphela ngokuphathelele kwiintlobo ezahlukeneyo zezityalo ezibhengezwe kwi Breeders ' Rights Act , 1976 ( UmThetho wamaLungelo abaMilisi beziTyalo , 1976 ) . .
Iintlobo zezityalo ezinokuba ngama ziqukiwe kuluhlu lwezityalo ( Table 1 ) ezinganikelwa ngokuphathelele kumalungelo abamilisi bezityalo . .
Umbhalisi wamaLungelo abaMilisi beziTyalo unokuthatha uhlobo oluthile njengohlobo olutsha aze anikele ngamalungelo abamilisi bezityalo xa : .
Izixhobo zokumilisa olo hlobo zingekathengiswa apha eMzantsi Afrika kwithuba elingaphaya konyaka . .
Kwimeko yohlobo lomthi okanye umdiliya , apho izixhobo zokumilisa zingekafumaneki kwelinye ilizwe , kwezoshishino okanye kuluntu kwithuba elingaphaya kweminyaka emithandathu , okanye kwimeko yesityalo nasiphi na esinye , kwithuba elingaphaya kweminyaka emine . .
Kufuneka izixhobo zokumilisa zihambelane ne ( distinctness , uniformity and stability ) ( i etolikwa ngokuthi kukucaca , ukufana nokuzinza ) : .
kufuneka sahluke ngokucacileyo kuhlobo naluphi na olunye lomnombo ofanayo .
kufuneka sifane , kukuthi , zonke izityalo kulimo kufuneka zikhangeleke zifana yaye zibe neempawu ezifanayo .
kufuneka sizinze , kukuthi , kufuneka izityalo zohlobo oluthile , emva kokulinywa amatyeli aliqela , zisoloko zikhangeleka zifana nezityalo zentsusa .
kufuneka sibe negama elamkelekileyo . .
Jonga uLuhlu 1 lwe Breeders ' Rights Act ( UmThetho wamaLungelo abaMilisi beziTyalo ) ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ingaba uhlobo lwesityalo sodidi oluswela ukhuselo , lupapashiwe kusini na . .
Xa uhlobo lwesityalo lungabonakali kuluhlu , thumela isicelo ngokuphathelele kupapasho kwakunye nenkxaso ebhaliweyo kuMbhalisi wamLungelo abaMilisi beziTyalo . .
Ukuba uhlobo lwesityalo lukhona kuluhlu , kufuneka kuthunyelwe izinto ezilandelayo : .
ifomu yesicelo ezaliswe ngokupheleleyo .
technical questionnaire ( Uthotho lwemibuzo yobuchwepheshe ) .
intlawulo emiselweyo yesicelo novavanyo .
imbewu okanye izixhobo zokumilisa .
ugunyaziso olubhaliweyo oluvela kumnini , ukuba awusimilisanga , wasikhetha okanye waqhubela phambili udidi . .
Bona ngendlela ecacileyo kuthotho lwemibuzo ukuba udidi olutsha kufuneka luthelekiswa neziphi ezinye iindidi ezaziwayo ukumisela ukuzibalula . .
Ungenza isicelo sokhuselo lwethutyana lodidi . .
Oku kuxela ukuthi udidi lukhuselwe ngethuba lovavanyo . .
Kufuneka unikezele ngokuzibophelela kokubhaliweyo ukuthi ungathengisi ( ngaphandle kwenjongo yokumilisa okanye uvavanyo ) nayiphi na into yokumilisa yodidi okujoliswe kulo kude kube zonke iimvavanyo zigqityiwe yaye kunikelwe ngamalungelo abamilisi . .
Luyakhuthazwa ukhuselo lwethutyana ngokuphathelele kwizityalo apho iimvavanyo zithatha ixesha elingaphaya konyaka ukuze zigqitywe . .
Kukho iintsuku ezimiselweyo ekufuneka kuthunyelwe ngazo amaxwebhu nezixhobo zokumilisa kuMbhalisi . .
Iinkcukacha zezi ntsuku , inani lezixhobo zokumilisa ekufuneka zithunyelwe nalapho kufuneka zithunyelwe khona , ziyafumaneka kuMbhalisi . .
Xa uluhlu lodidi lukhona ngokuphathelele kolo hlobo olwenzelwa isicelo samalungelo abamilisi bezityalo , thumela izicelo ngaxeshanye ukulondoloza ixesha nemali . .
Konke ukutya kwasefama okungeniswe elizweni , okwenziweyo , okuvelisiweyo okanye okuthengiswayo apha eMzantsi Afrika kufuneka kubhaliswe ku ( Umbhalisi ) , Act 36 of 1947 ( UmThetho 36 wowe ) . .
Umenzi wesicelo kufuneka kube ngumntu ngokusemthethweni , umzekelo , John Peter Citizen T/A Diepsloot Stud . .
Inkampani ya phesheya ayifanelanga ukwenza isicelo sokungenisa elizweni apha eMzantsi Afrika . .
Isicelo sokubhalisa ukutya kwasefama nezichumiso singenziwa kuphela yinkampani yasekhaya ebhalisiweyo , ummi waseMzantsi Afrika okanye umbutho osemthethweni obhalisiweyo apha eMzantsi Afrika . .
Ukutya kwasefama kuquka umququ , amakhatshu , ifula engasilwanga , ifula yovimba , nayiphi na isirili eziinkozo okanye ukutya okulungiswe ngumnini ngenjongo yokuzisebenzisela kona . .
Cela ii ( izikhokelo ) malunga neemfuno ngokubanzi zokutya kwasefama kuMbhalisi , Act 36 of 1947 ( UmThetho 36 wowe ) . .
Isicelo sokubhalisa ukutya kwasefama siqulethe : .
Incwadi echazayo evela kumnini wobhaliso okanye ummeli otyunjiweyo . .
Ileta echazayo kufuneka iquke : .
igama lemveliso .
inombolo yobhaliso xa imveliso sele ibhalisiwe .
isizathu sokuthumela isicelo ( ukuthi sisicelo esitsha , isicelo sokulungisa , isicelo sokubhalisa imveliso ezalwa lubhaliso olukhoyo ) .
iileta zesivumelwano xa kufuneka imvume yominini wobhaliso ( imvume yokubhalisa imveliso ezalwa lubhaliso olukhoyo okanye imvume yokusebenzisa igama lemveliso yenye inkampani kwileyibhile ) .
intlawulo echanekileyo yesicelo .
iitsheki ezithunyelwa ngokwahlukeneyo nesicelo kufuneka zikhatshwe yileta echazayo . .
Iitsheki neposoda kufuneka zihlawulwe ku : Agricultur . .
Thumela iifomu ( iikopi ezimbini ) zesicelo zezicelo ezitsha nezilungiso kubhaliso olukhoyo , kuquka neenguqu zokwakheka . .
Zalisa ngokupheleleyo , ngaphandle kokubhekisa kwizicelo zexesha elidlulileyo , iinombolo zamaphepha okanye ezinye iimveliso ( okungenani ikopi enye yeefomu zesicelo kufuneka ibe nentsayino yentsusa . .
Enye inokuba yikopi ) . .
Iifomu zesicelo kufuneka zisayinwe ngumntu otyunjiweyo ngokusemthethweni yaye lo kunqweneleka kube ngumntu wenkampani onoqhagamshelwano noMbhalisi . .
Igama nenombolo yobhaliso yemveliso kufuneka lisetyenziswe njengoko kuchaziwe kwisiqinisekiso sobhaliso . .
Nayiphi na inguqu egameni , nokuba incinci kangakanani , iya kuthathwa njengesilungiso . .
Iifomu zesicelo kufuneka zifakwe kwiofisi yolawulo . .
Ukunikela izicelo kwii- Technical Advisers ( Abacebisi bezoBuchwepheshe ) kuya kubambezela inkqubo . .
Ukulobela ulonwabo kukwenza imisebenzi emalunga nokuloba efana nokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yolonwabo . .
Ukuze ungenise iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yolonwabo ( recreational basis ) , kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle nesivunywa nguMphathiswa weSebe lokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho ( Minister of Environmental Affairs and Tourism ( DEA&T ) okanye omnye umntu onegunya lokwenza oko . .
Iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle mazingathengiswa , kodwa mazisetyenziselwe injongo yokuba zityiwe okanye zisetyenziswe . .
Akukho mntu uya kungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngaphandle kwepemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi ngenjongo yolonwabo . .
Kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi entsha yokungenisa intlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yolonwabo xa leyo ibikho iphelelwe . .
Ukungaphumeleli ukubambelela kule miqathango yepemithi kunganeziphumo zokunqunyanyiswa okanye ukurhoxiswa kwepemithi . .
NB : Le pemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ayibandakanyi iintlanzi zamanzi afreshi nezilawulwa liSebe lezoLimo . .
Izicelo zeepemithi zokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ukulungiselela iintlanzi zamanzi afreshi ziphilile okanye iintlanzi i fish mazenziwe kwiSebe lezoLimo . .
Kusetyenziswa le miqathango izizithintelo ukungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle : .
Akukhozi zidweliswe kuluhlu lweentlobo ( species ) zamazwe angaphandle emazingeniswe kweli lizwe . .
( Ukuba ufuna ingcaciso engaphezulu ngeentlobo ze of International Trade in Endangered Species ( CITES ) yiya kwiziko lewebhu http://www.cites.org . .
IiPemithi zokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yolonwabo ezikhutshelwa ukulungiselela ukusetyenziswa ngabantu okanye ukutyiwa ziya kuba semthethweni kangangethuba lolo hambo lokuya nokubuya kwilizwe ekuyiwa kulo . .
Akukho zintlanzi zolwandle zihleliyo zamazwe angaphandle zingangeniswa kweli lizwe . .
Zalisa iifom zokwenza isicelo ezifanelekileyo uze uzingenise kwiSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho , kunye nale ngcaciso ilandelayo : .
imihla yokumka nokubuyela eMzantsi Afrika .
igama lelizwe ekuyiwa kulo .
malichazwe iziko eliyi yemida yaseMzantsi Afrika eya kusetyenziswa xa kubuyelwa eMzantsi Afrika .
ubungqina bedilesi yendawo yokuhlala , iinombolo zefowuni neenombolo zefeksi zaseMzantsi Afrika .
cacisa ukuba iintlanzi ziya kungeniswa zinjani na kweli lizwe ( Zikhenkciwe / Zibandisiwe / njl.njl. ) .
ikopi engqiniweyo yesazisi somenzi ngamnye .
ubungqina bentlawulo ( isiliphu sedipozithi yebhanki sentlawulo yepemithi ye ngomenzi ngamnye ) .
akukho zifeksi , zikopi nee , ziya kwamkelwa .
iifom zingangeniswa ngesandla okanye ngokuthunyelwa ngeposi . .
Nceda uqaphele : .
Yenza isicelo ubuncinane kwiiveki ezimbini phambi kokumka kwakho ukuvumela ithuba lokusingathwa kwaso .
Akukho pemithi ifunekayo ukwenzela ibheyithi yokuthiya . .
Nangona kunjalo , nceda uqinisekise ukuba unayo ipemithi nokuba yeyebheyithi yokulobela ulonwabo ( kuphela ngumthwalo oqingqiweyo wengxowa yemihla ngemihla ongahanjiswayo ) ikheshi yebheyithi ethengiweyo . .
Ukulobela ukurhweba kukwenza umsebenzi onxulumene nokuloba ofana nokuthumela iintlanzi zolwandle kumazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yokuzithengisa . .
Ukuze uthumele iintlanzi zolwandle kumazwe angaphandle okanye ngaphandle kwemida yeRiphablikhi yoMzantsi Afrika , kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi yokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle nesivunywa nguMphathiswa weSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho ( Minister of Environmental Affairs and Tourism okanye omnye umntu onegunya lokwenza oko . .
Akukho mntu uya kuthumela iintlanzi zolwandle kumazwe angaphandle ngaphandle kwepemithi . .
Xa ipemithi yokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle ebikho iphelelelwe emva kweenyanga ezintathu , kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi entsha . .
Ukungaphumeleli ukubambelela kwimiqathango yepemithi kunganeziphumo zokunqunyanyiswa okanye ukurhoxiswa kwepemithi . .
NB : Le pemithi yokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle ayizibandakanyi iintlanzi zamanzi afreshi nelawulwa liSebe lezoLimo . .
Izicelo zeepemithi zokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle ukulungiselela iintlanzi zamanzi afreshi ziphilile okanye iintlanzi i fish mazenziwe kwiSebe lezoLimo . .
Iintlobo ezikuluhlu lwe of International Trade in Endangered Species ( CITES ) azinakungeniswa kweli lizwe . .
( Ukuba ufuna ingcaciso engaphezulu nge yiya kwiziko lewebhu http://www.cites.org . .
Ipemithi yokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle yohlobo lweentlanzi ezifana ne mayihanjiswe nesatifikethi se kumthwalo ngamnye . .
Iipemithi zokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle ezikhutshelwa ezi ntlobo : bigeye tuna , southern bluefin tuna , swordfish , Antarctic toothfish , ne toothfish , mazihanjiswe kunye noxwebhu olufanelekileyo oluneenkcukacha zokulotyiweyo ( relevant catch statistical document ) kumthwalo ngamnye . .
Amaxwebhu eenkcukacha zokulotyiweyo ( Catch statistical documents ) ayafumaneka kwiSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho , iSebe le and Coastal Management , iCandelo le and High Seas Fisheries Management . .
Yenza isicelo sepemithi yokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle . .
Fumana ifom yokwenza isicelo ngokuthumela isicelo kwi iMarine and Coastal Management Office ( jonga iinkcukacha zoqhagamshelwano apha ngezantsi ) okanye kwi elisebe yeSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho ( Department of Environmental Affairs and Tourism okanye uyikhuphele kwa : http://www.mcm ifom yokwenza isicelo ngononophelo uze uqinisekise ukuba uyazanelisa iimfuneko nemiqathango .
Nikezela ngale ngcaciso ilandelayo : .
iidilesi zendawo yokuhlala zabantu abangenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle kwelo lizwe ziya kulo .
amagama awaziwayo nangawenzululwazi eentlobo zeentlanzi .
ubungakanani beentlobo eziza kuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle .
kwimeko yaxa kukho i ebandakanyekayo , kufuneka kuqhotyoshelwe isivumelwano phakathi kwamaqela achaphazelekayo amabini kunye neekopi zezazisi zabo banelungelo lokusayina .
iikopi zamaxwebhu eenkcukacha zokulotyiweyo kufuneka zibonelelwe kuzo zonke iintlobo ze tuna , southern bluefin tuna , swordfish , Antarctic toothfish , ne toothfish ezithunyelwe phantsi kwepemithi yokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle yethuba langaphambili . .
Ukuba umenzi wepemithi yokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle akanguye umnikazi onelungelo lokuloba , makanikezele ngala maxwebhu alandelayo : .
ubungqina beedilesi zendawo yokuhlala zabathengisi beentlanzi zolwandle eziza kuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle .
amagama awaziwayo nangawenzululwazi eentlobo zeentlanzi eziza kuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle .
ubungakanani beentlobo eziza kuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle . .
Ngenisa iikopi ezingqiniweyo zala maxwebhu alandelayo : .
ikopi engqiniweyo yesazisi esiyintsusa namaxwebhu okubhalisa enkampani yakho , nenkampani ezizii corporation okanye iitrasti .
iikopi ezingqiniweyo zeepemithi ezisemthethweni zokungenisa iintlanzi ezivela kwiSebe loRhwebo noShishino i of Trade and Industry okanye izaziso zeepemithi .
iikopi ezingqiniweyo ( certified copies ) zesatifikethi esiyintsusa i Clearance Certificate njengoko sivunywe saza sakhutshwa yiNkonzo yeNgeniso yaseMzantsi Afrika . .
Yazisa isebe elikufutshane lakwa African Bureau of Standards ( SABS ) malunga nomthwalo wakho oza kuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle ukuba iintlanzi oza kuzithumela azikhofreshi kwaye azinako ukutyiwa . .
Ukuba iintlanzi zifreshi kwaye zilungiselelwe ukutyiwa yazisa i of Health . .
Intlawulo yokwenza isicelo eyi ( equka konke ) iyafuneka . .
Zalisa , uze usayine uze uthumele ifom yokwenza isicelo sepemithi yokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle kunye namaxwebhu ayimfuneko kwi and Coastal Management Office . .
( Jonga idilesi engasezantsi ) . .
Izicelo zentsusa mazithunyelwe ngeposi , ukuze ingakhutshwa ipemithi xa ungakwenzanga oko . .
Ukungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yokurhweba kuthetha ukuba wenza imisebenzi efana nokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yokurhweba ngazo . .
Ukuze ungenise iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle , kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle nesivunywa nguMphathiswa weMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho okanye umntu onegunya lokwenza oko . .
Akukho mntu uya kurhweba angenise iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngaphandle kwepemithi . .
Yenza isicelo sepemithi entsha yokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle xa leyo ubunayo iphelelwe lixesha . .
Ukungaphumeleli ukubambelela kwimiqathango yepemithi kunganeziphumo zokunqunyanyiswa okanye ukurhoxiswa kwayo . .
NB : Le pemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ayibandakanyi iintlanzi yamanzi afreshi nezilawulwa liSebe lezoLimo . .
Izicelo zeepemithi zokungenisa iintlanzi ngaphakathi kweli lizwe ukulungiselela iintlanzi zamanzi afreshi ziphilile okanye iintlanzi i fish mazenziwe kwiSebe lezoLimo . .
Kusetyenziswa le miqathango izizithintelo yokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle : .
Iintlobo ezikuluhlu lwe of International Trade in Endangered Species ( CITES ) zamazwe angaphandle azinakungeniswa kweli lizwe . .
( Ukuba ufuna ingcaciso engaphezulu nge yiya kwiziko lewebhu http://www.cites.org . .
Ipemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ezifana ne , rock lobster nezinye iintlobo ezimiselwe kuMthetho i Living Resources Act , No . 18 , 1998 ( MLRA ) Appendix 4 , 5 & 12 , iya kuba semthethweni ukulungiselela umthwalo ngamnye ( iiveki ezintathu ukususela kumhla wokukhutshwa kwayo ) . .
Kuphela ngunonkala okhenkciweyo opheleleyo ( okanye amaqhekeza akhe anobunzima be g okanye ngaphezulu nangekho ngaphezu kweetoni eziyi anokungeniswa amazwe angaphandle ( qho ngonyaka ) . .
Akukho nonkala uhleliyo welizwe langaphandle unokungeniswa kweli lizwe . .
Fumana ifom yokwenza isicelo ngokuthumela isicelo kwi i and Coastal Management Office ( jonga iinkcukacha zoqhagamshelwano apha ngezantsi ) okanye kwi elisebe yeSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho okanye uyikhuphele kwiziko lewebhu : http://www.mcm .

iidilesi zendawo yokuhlala zabantu abathumela iintlanzi apha kwilizwe lokuzalwa .

ubungakanani beentlobo eziza kungeniswa zamazwe angaphandle . .
Ngenisa isicelo sakho kunye nala maxwebhu alandelayo : .
ikopi engqiniweyo yesazisi esiyintsusa namaxwebhu okubhalisa enkampani yakho , nenkampani ezizii corporation okanye iitrasti . .
iikopi ezingqiniweyo zeepemithi ezisemthethweni zokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle kwiSebe lezoRhwebo noShishino i of Trade and Industry ) okanye izaziso zeepemithi . .
iikopi ezingqiniweyo zesatifikethi esiyintsusa i Clearance Certificate njengoko sivunywe saza sakhutshwa yiNkonzo yeNgeniso yaseMzantsi Afrika . .
Yazisa isebe elikufutshane lakwa African Bureau of Standards ( SABS ) ngokumalunga nomthwalo ongeniswayo wamazwe angaphandle xa ngaba iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle azikho freshi kwaye azilungiselelwanga ukutyiwa ngabantu . .

( Jonga idilesi apha ngezantsi ) .
Iifom eziyintsusa mazithunyelwe ngeposi , kwaye ukungakwenzi oko , kuya kubangela ukuba ipemithi ingakhutshwa . .
Intlawulo yokwenza isicelo eyi ( incl . ) iyafuneka . .
Ungacela ukuba imali ehlawulelwa inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu ( isapoti ) sitshintshwe , ngenxa yokuba asaneli okanye ngenxa yokuba uyoyisakala ukukhupha loo mali yesapoti . .
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi , yiya kwiSebe lezoBulungisa noPhuhliso loMgaqo .
Inkqubo emayilandelwe .
Ukubangaba ungulo mntu ufumana isapoti : .
Yenza isicelo kwinkundla kamantyi ekwisithili apho lo mntu uhlawula isapoti ahlala khona . .
Gcwalisa ifom yesicelo efanelekileyo uze uyihambise kwigosa lesapoti , ikunye nesitetimenti sengeniso kunye nenkcitho . .
Ukubangaba ungulo mntu uhlawula isapoti kodwa iyakoyisa le mali uyikhuphayo : .
Yenza isicelo sokulungiswa komyalelo kwi kamantyi ekwisithili ekuhlala kuso lo mntu umsapotayo . .
Gcwalisa ifom ebandakanyekayo kwaye uyihambise kwigosa lesapoti . .
Hambisa isitetimenti esipheleleyo sengeniso kunye nenkcitho , ndawonye nengxelo echaza izizathu zesicelo , kwigosa lesapoti , akukhathaliseki nokuba ungumzuzi okanye ungumhlawuli wemali yesapoti . .
Kuyakuthi ke kulandelwe inkqubo efanayo naxa kufakwa isibango sesapoti . .
Imithetho esetyenziswayo .
UMthetho weNkxaso yokuNakekela omnye umntu , kunye neMigqaliselo eyayamene nawo .
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo .
Uyakuphathwa ngokulinganayo , ngokunobuntu , nangesidima nentlonipho . .
Isicelo sakho siyakuphathwa ngokukhawuleza nangobunono kangangoko kunokwenzeka .
Faka nasiphina isikhalazo onganaso kuMphandi weNkxaso yokuNakekela omnye umntu ( weSapoti ) , kwiGosa leNkxaso yokuNakekela omnye umntu , kuManejala weNkundla , kwiNtloko yeNgingqi kwezoBulungisa noPhuhliso loMgaqo okanye kwiZiko leNkonzo eGqwesileyo ; kwiProjekthi yeNkxaso yokuNakekela omnye umntu yeSebe leLizwe lezoBulungisa noPhuhliso loMgaqo ; okanye kwiCandelo loBuqondisi beMibandela ye . .
Iindleko .
Ngaphandle kokuba igosa elihambisa imiyalelo yenkundla ( i ) licela kuqale kukhutshwe imali , ukuze likwazi ukukhupha umyalelo wokuhlawula isapoti , iindleko ziyakubancinane okanye zingabikho konke konke . .
Njengoko inkqubo yokubhalisa inkampani enobutyebi bezinto kunye neemali zezabelo inzima , kwenziwa isiphakamiso sokuba abenzi basebenzise iinkonzo zamagqwetha . .
UMqulu oBhaliweyo kunye neMimiselo yenkampani kufuneka ziqulunqwe kwaye zilungelelaniselwe ukufanelana nenkampani enobutyebi bezinto kunye neemali zezabelo kwaye ziqinisekiswe ligosa loluntu elinegunya lasemthethweni lokungqina imiqulu neengxelo ezifungelweyo , kwaye elingumnntu oqeqeshiweyo ngokwasemthethweni . .
Inkampani yoluntu ingasebenzisa uLuhlu A kwifom yesicelo ngokupheleleyo okanye iyilungelelanise neemeko zayo , xa ngaba nje ihambisana nomThetho weeNkampani . .
Inkampani yabucala ingasebenzisa uLuhlu B kwifom yesicelo ngokupheleleyo okanye iyilungelelanise neemeko zayo , xa ngaba nje ihambisana nomThetho weeNkampani . .
